\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01454}01454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ safe\ API\ to\ ensure\ interrupt\ entry\ is\ as\ fast\ and\ as\ simple\ as\ possible.}}
